			<div class="post-6168 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-my-tutorials category-quicknote-analysis-of-pandora-ransomware tag-bochs tag-ida tag-malware-analysis tag-pandora tag-ransomware tag-reverseengineering tag-x64dbg" id="post-6168">
				<div class="posttitle">
					<h2 class="pagetitle">[QuickNote] Analysis of Pandora&nbsp;ransomware</h2>
					<small>
						Posted: March 21, 2022 in <a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/category/my-tutorials/" rel="category tag">My Tutorials</a>, <a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/category/my-tutorials/quicknote-analysis-of-pandora-ransomware/" rel="category tag">[QuickNote] Analysis of Pandora ransomware</a>						<br />
						Tags: <a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/tag/bochs/" rel="tag">Bochs</a>, <a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/tag/ida/" rel="tag">IDA</a>, <a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/tag/malware-analysis/" rel="tag">Malware Analysis</a>, <a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/tag/pandora/" rel="tag">Pandora</a>, <a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/tag/ransomware/" rel="tag">Ransomware</a>, <a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/tag/reverseengineering/" rel="tag">ReverseEngineering</a>, <a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/tag/x64dbg/" rel="tag">x64dbg</a>					</small>
				</div>
									<div class="postcomments"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/2022/03/21/quicknote-analysis-of-pandora-ransomware/#comments">1</a></div>
								<div class="entry">
					<div class="cs-rating pd-rating" id="pd_rating_holder_1003814_post_6168"></div><br/>
<p class="has-vivid-red-color has-text-color"><strong>FOREWORD:</strong></p>



<ul class="wp-block-list"><li><em>Pandora&#8217;s code looks very weird and obfuscate complicated, so this analysis does not cover all its functions.</em></li><li><em>I&#8217;m not a crypto expert, so I won&#8217;t dive into Pandora&#8217;s function like </em><em>generating encryption key</em>, <em>process of creating threads to do its main task of encrypting files</em>, <em>writing file footer</em>,..</li><li><em>During malware code analysis, I found that <strong>Pandora </strong>and <strong>Rook </strong>ransomware (<a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://chuongdong.com/reverse%20engineering/2022/01/06/RookRansomware" target="_blank">https://chuongdong.com/reverse%20engineering/2022/01/06/RookRansomware</a></em>)<em> shared a lot of similarities.</em></li></ul>



<p></p>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading">1. Pandora sample</h4>



<p>The analyzed sample is a 64-bit executable: <a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://www.virustotal.com/gui/file/5b56c5d86347e164c6e571c86dbf5b1535eae6b979fede6ed66b01e79ea33b7b/details" target="_blank">0c4a84b66832a08dccc42b478d9d5e1b</a></p>



<span id="more-6168"></span>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading">2. Manual unpacking</h4>



<p class="has-text-align-justify">Quick check the sample with some tools like <strong>ExeInfo PE</strong>, <strong>DiE</strong>, all results show that this sample is packed by <strong>UPX</strong>.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image1.png"><img data-attachment-id="6173" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image1/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image1.png" data-orig-size="1022,291" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image1" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image1.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image1.png?w=1022" width="1022" height="291" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image1.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6173" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image1.png 1022w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image1.png?w=128&amp;h=36 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image1.png?w=300&amp;h=85 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image1.png?w=768&amp;h=219 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1022px) 100vw, 1022px" /></a></figure></div>


<p class="has-text-align-justify">Checking more information about sections shows that the names of sections have been changed, not <strong>UPX0</strong>, <strong>UPX1</strong>, it changed to <strong>pppp </strong>and <strong>cccc</strong>.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image2.png"><img data-attachment-id="6174" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image2/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image2.png" data-orig-size="1146,143" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image2" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image2.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image2.png?w=1146" width="1146" height="143" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image2.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6174" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image2.png 1146w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image2.png?w=128&amp;h=16 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image2.png?w=300&amp;h=37 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image2.png?w=768&amp;h=96 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image2.png?w=1024&amp;h=128 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1146px) 100vw, 1146px" /></a></figure>



<p>Additionally, the information behind the <strong>3.00 UPX!</strong> strings were stripped by the attacker:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image3.png"><img data-attachment-id="6176" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image3/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image3.png" data-orig-size="628,244" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image3" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image3.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image3.png?w=628" width="628" height="244" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image3.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6176" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image3.png 628w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image3.png?w=128&amp;h=50 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image3.png?w=300&amp;h=117 300w" sizes="(max-width: 628px) 100vw, 628px" /></a></figure></div>


<p>Therefore, we can not use the<strong> <code>upx -d</code></strong> command to auto unpack this sample:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image4.png"><img data-attachment-id="6178" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image4/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image4.png" data-orig-size="936,345" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image4" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image4.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image4.png?w=936" loading="lazy" width="936" height="345" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image4.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6178" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image4.png 936w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image4.png?w=128&amp;h=47 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image4.png?w=300&amp;h=111 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image4.png?w=768&amp;h=283 768w" sizes="(max-width: 936px) 100vw, 936px" /></a></figure></div>


<p>For manually unpacking, I used <strong>x64dbg </strong>to find OEP and <strong>Scylla </strong>to dump the file and fix the IAT:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image5.png"><img data-attachment-id="6180" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image5/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image5.png" data-orig-size="590,478" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image5" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image5.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image5.png?w=590" loading="lazy" width="590" height="478" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image5.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6180" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image5.png 590w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image5.png?w=118&amp;h=96 118w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image5.png?w=300&amp;h=243 300w" sizes="(max-width: 590px) 100vw, 590px" /></a></figure></div>


<p>Here is the unpacked file that can run normally: <a href="https://www.virustotal.com/gui/file/0fac541a5613a69dd16690d16ebf4b2fad3ac4fc86b9b5f8fd715a003c027a1e/details" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">1497ac198a13de8c4e6d1a1e73eaa50f</a></p>



<p></p>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading">3. Pandora Code Obfuscation</h4>



<p></p>



<p>Pandora developer makes it very difficult for static analysis, its code uses indirect calls through registers <strong><code>rax, rdx, rbp</code></strong>, etc. Important strings such as <em><strong>Mutex name, Dll Name, PUBLIC KEY info, Ransom note,</strong></em> are already encrypted and decrypted when the malicious code executes.</p>



<p>Related to indirect calls, it can be seen as follows:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list"><li>The calls to the decrypt string function will take the <strong><code>rdx </code></strong>and <strong><code>rcx </code></strong>registers as parameters. The <strong><code>rdx </code></strong>register will point to the memory area containing the encrypted string. The <strong><code>rcx </code></strong>register will point to the memory area containing the decoded string.</li></ul>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image6.png"><img data-attachment-id="6184" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image6/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image6.png" data-orig-size="771,229" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image6" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image6.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image6.png?w=771" loading="lazy" width="771" height="229" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image6.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6184" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image6.png 771w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image6.png?w=128&amp;h=38 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image6.png?w=300&amp;h=89 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image6.png?w=768&amp;h=228 768w" sizes="(max-width: 771px) 100vw, 771px" /></a></figure></div>


<ul class="wp-block-list"><li>The calls to the API functions or Pandora&#8217;s function should look like this:</li></ul>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image7.png"><img data-attachment-id="6186" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image7/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image7.png" data-orig-size="1044,316" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image7" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image7.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image7.png?w=1044" loading="lazy" width="1044" height="316" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image7.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6186" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image7.png 1044w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image7.png?w=128&amp;h=39 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image7.png?w=300&amp;h=91 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image7.png?w=768&amp;h=232 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image7.png?w=1024&amp;h=310 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1044px) 100vw, 1044px" /></a></figure></div>


<p class="has-text-align-justify">Besides, Pandora also applies control flow obfuscation technique. For example, the pseudo-code of  function that decrypt the string is as follows:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image8.png"><img data-attachment-id="6188" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image8/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image8.png" data-orig-size="644,720" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image8" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image8.png?w=268" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image8.png?w=644" loading="lazy" width="644" height="720" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image8.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6188" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image8.png 644w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image8.png?w=86&amp;h=96 86w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image8.png?w=268&amp;h=300 268w" sizes="(max-width: 644px) 100vw, 644px" /></a></figure></div>


<p></p>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading">4. Analyze some of the main functions of Pandora</h4>



<p>To be able to analyze, I use IDA in combination with <strong>Bochs debugger</strong>.</p>



<p></p>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">4.1. Create Mutex</h5>



<ul class="wp-block-list"><li>First, Pandora decrypts the mutex name is “<strong><code>ThisIsMutexa</code></strong>”, then call the <strong><code>OpenMutexA </code></strong>function to check the existence of this mutex.</li></ul>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image9.png"><img data-attachment-id="6190" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image9/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image9.png" data-orig-size="2244,405" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image9" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image9.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image9.png?w=2244" loading="lazy" width="2244" height="405" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image9.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6190" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image9.png 2244w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image9.png?w=128&amp;h=23 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image9.png?w=300&amp;h=54 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image9.png?w=768&amp;h=139 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image9.png?w=1024&amp;h=185 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 2244px) 100vw, 2244px" /></a></figure></div>


<ul class="wp-block-list"><li>If the mutex has not been created, call the <strong><code>CreateMutexA </code></strong>function to create the mutex to ensure that only one instance of the malware is running in the system.</li></ul>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image10.png"><img data-attachment-id="6192" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image10/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image10.png" data-orig-size="1241,405" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image10" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image10.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image10.png?w=1241" loading="lazy" width="1241" height="405" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image10.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6192" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image10.png 1241w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image10.png?w=128&amp;h=42 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image10.png?w=300&amp;h=98 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image10.png?w=768&amp;h=251 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image10.png?w=1024&amp;h=334 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1241px) 100vw, 1241px" /></a></figure></div>


<p></p>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">4.2. Call NtSetInformationProcess</h5>



<p>Pandora decrypts the string &#8220;<strong><code>NtSetInformationProcess</code></strong>&#8220;, calls the <strong><code>GetProcAddress </code></strong>function to retrieve the address. Then call the function <code><strong>NtSetInformationProcess </strong></code>with the <strong><code>ProcessInformationClass </code></strong>parameter passed as “<strong><code>ProcessInstrumentationCallback</code></strong>”:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image11.png"><img data-attachment-id="6195" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image11/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image11.png" data-orig-size="1185,439" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image11" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image11.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image11.png?w=1185" loading="lazy" width="1185" height="439" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image11.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6195" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image11.png 1185w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image11.png?w=128&amp;h=47 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image11.png?w=300&amp;h=111 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image11.png?w=768&amp;h=285 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image11.png?w=1024&amp;h=379 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1185px) 100vw, 1185px" /></a></figure></div>


<p><em>I still do not know the purpose of using this function of Pandora.</em></p>



<p></p>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">4.3. Patching EtwEventWrite function</h5>



<p class="has-text-align-justify">To disable ETW logging, Pandora decrypts the string “<strong><code>EtwEventWrite</code></strong>” and uses <strong><code>GetProcAddress </code></strong>to get the address of the function. Then use <strong><code>WriteProcessMemory </code></strong>to replace the first byte of the <strong><code>EtwEventWrite </code></strong>function with the opcode <strong><code>0xC3 </code></strong>for the purpose to return immediately stopping the user-mode loggers.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image12.png"><img data-attachment-id="6198" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image12/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image12.png" data-orig-size="1320,1148" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image12" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image12.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image12.png?w=1320" loading="lazy" width="1320" height="1148" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image12.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6198" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image12.png 1320w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image12.png?w=110&amp;h=96 110w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image12.png?w=300&amp;h=261 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image12.png?w=768&amp;h=668 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image12.png?w=1024&amp;h=891 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1320px) 100vw, 1320px" /></a></figure></div>


<p></p>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">4.4. Defeat AmsiScanBuffer function</h5>



<p>Pandora decrypts the string “<strong><code>amsi.dll</code></strong>” and calls the <strong><code>GetModuleHandleA </code></strong>function to get the <strong><code>amsi </code></strong>handle.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image13.png"><img data-attachment-id="6200" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image13/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image13.png" data-orig-size="1106,436" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image13" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image13.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image13.png?w=1106" loading="lazy" width="1106" height="436" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image13.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6200" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image13.png 1106w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image13.png?w=128&amp;h=50 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image13.png?w=300&amp;h=118 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image13.png?w=768&amp;h=303 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image13.png?w=1024&amp;h=404 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1106px) 100vw, 1106px" /></a></figure></div>


<p class="has-text-align-justify">Decrypts the string &#8220;<strong><code>AmsiScanBuffer</code></strong>&#8221; and get the address of the function. Then use <strong><code>VirtualProtectEx </code></strong>to change the protection at the <strong><code>AmsiScanBuffer</code></strong>.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image14.png"><img data-attachment-id="6202" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image14/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image14.png" data-orig-size="1151,1029" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image14" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image14.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image14.png?w=1151" loading="lazy" width="1151" height="1029" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image14.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6202" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image14.png 1151w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image14.png?w=107&amp;h=96 107w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image14.png?w=300&amp;h=268 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image14.png?w=768&amp;h=687 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image14.png?w=1024&amp;h=915 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1151px) 100vw, 1151px" /></a></figure></div>


<p></p>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">4.5. Generate RSA key</h5>



<p class="has-text-align-justify">Pandora decrypts the string &#8220;<code><strong>fast_test</strong></code>&#8220;, then uses the <strong><code>CryptAcquireContext</code></strong>, <strong><code>CryptGenRandom </code></strong>functions to generate a random bytes buffer:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image15.png"><img data-attachment-id="6205" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image15/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image15.png" data-orig-size="1150,209" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image15" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image15.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image15.png?w=1150" loading="lazy" width="1150" height="209" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image15.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6205" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image15.png 1150w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image15.png?w=128&amp;h=23 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image15.png?w=300&amp;h=55 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image15.png?w=768&amp;h=140 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image15.png?w=1024&amp;h=186 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1150px) 100vw, 1150px" /></a></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image16.png"><img data-attachment-id="6206" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image16/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image16.png" data-orig-size="786,309" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image16" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image16.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image16.png?w=786" loading="lazy" width="786" height="309" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image16.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6206" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image16.png 786w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image16.png?w=128&amp;h=50 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image16.png?w=300&amp;h=118 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image16.png?w=768&amp;h=302 768w" sizes="(max-width: 786px) 100vw, 786px" /></a></figure></div>


<p class="has-text-align-justify">Pandora calls the function to decrypt the RSA public key. Then call the <strong><code>mbedtls_pk_parse_public_key </code></strong>function to parse this public key:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image17.png"><img data-attachment-id="6208" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image17/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image17.png" data-orig-size="1708,543" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image17" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image17.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image17.png?w=1708" loading="lazy" width="1708" height="543" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image17.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6208" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image17.png 1708w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image17.png?w=128&amp;h=41 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image17.png?w=300&amp;h=95 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image17.png?w=768&amp;h=244 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image17.png?w=1024&amp;h=326 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1708px) 100vw, 1708px" /></a></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_public_key_info.png"><img data-attachment-id="6250" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/decrypt_public_key_info/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_public_key_info.png" data-orig-size="1836,784" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="decrypt_public_key_info" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_public_key_info.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_public_key_info.png?w=1836" loading="lazy" width="1836" height="784" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_public_key_info.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6250" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_public_key_info.png 1836w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_public_key_info.png?w=128&amp;h=55 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_public_key_info.png?w=300&amp;h=128 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_public_key_info.png?w=768&amp;h=328 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_public_key_info.png?w=1024&amp;h=437 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1836px) 100vw, 1836px" /></a></figure></div>


<p>The decrypted content of the Public key is as follows:</p>


<div class="wp-block-syntaxhighlighter-code "><pre class="brush: cpp; title: ; notranslate" title="">
-----BEGIN PUBLIC KEY-----

</pre></div>


<p></p>



<p class="has-text-align-justify">Use the <strong><code>RegCreateKeyExW </code></strong>function to open the “<strong><code>Software</code></strong>” subkey in the <strong><code>HKEY_CURRENT_USER</code></strong> branch.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image18.png"><img data-attachment-id="6210" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image18/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image18.png" data-orig-size="1325,402" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image18" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image18.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image18.png?w=1325" loading="lazy" width="1325" height="402" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image18.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6210" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image18.png 1325w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image18.png?w=128&amp;h=39 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image18.png?w=300&amp;h=91 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image18.png?w=768&amp;h=233 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image18.png?w=1024&amp;h=311 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1325px) 100vw, 1325px" /></a></figure></div>


<p>Then call the <strong><code>RegQueryValueExW </code></strong>function to check if the registry value “<strong><code>Public</code></strong>” exists in there:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image19.png"><img data-attachment-id="6212" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image19/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image19.png" data-orig-size="1247,293" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image19" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image19.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image19.png?w=1247" loading="lazy" width="1247" height="293" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image19.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6212" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image19.png 1247w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image19.png?w=128&amp;h=30 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image19.png?w=300&amp;h=70 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image19.png?w=768&amp;h=180 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image19.png?w=1024&amp;h=241 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1247px) 100vw, 1247px" /></a></figure></div>


<p>If it does not, the malware generates a public-private key pair for the victim.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image20.png"><img data-attachment-id="6213" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image20/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image20.png" data-orig-size="1221,306" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image20" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image20.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image20.png?w=1221" loading="lazy" width="1221" height="306" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image20.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6213" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image20.png 1221w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image20.png?w=128&amp;h=32 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image20.png?w=300&amp;h=75 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image20.png?w=768&amp;h=192 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image20.png?w=1024&amp;h=257 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1221px) 100vw, 1221px" /></a></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image21.png"><img data-attachment-id="6214" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image21/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image21.png" data-orig-size="1195,604" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image21" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image21.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image21.png?w=1195" loading="lazy" width="1195" height="604" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image21.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6214" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image21.png 1195w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image21.png?w=128&amp;h=65 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image21.png?w=300&amp;h=152 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image21.png?w=768&amp;h=388 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image21.png?w=1024&amp;h=518 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1195px) 100vw, 1195px" /></a></figure></div>


<p></p>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">4.6. Update shutdown priority</h5>



<p>Pandora calls the <strong><code>SetProcessShutdownParameters </code></strong>function to sets a shutdown order:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image22.png"><img data-attachment-id="6216" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image22/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image22.png" data-orig-size="1531,156" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image22" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image22.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image22.png?w=1531" loading="lazy" width="1531" height="156" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image22.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6216" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image22.png 1531w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image22.png?w=128&amp;h=13 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image22.png?w=300&amp;h=31 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image22.png?w=768&amp;h=78 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image22.png?w=1024&amp;h=104 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1531px) 100vw, 1531px" /></a></figure></div>


<p></p>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">4.7. Empty all Recycle Bins on all drives</h5>



<p>For empty all recycle bins, Pandora calls the function <strong><code>SHEmptyRecycleBinA</code></strong>:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image23.png"><img data-attachment-id="6218" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image23/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image23.png" data-orig-size="1244,171" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image23" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image23.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image23.png?w=1244" loading="lazy" width="1244" height="171" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image23.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6218" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image23.png 1244w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image23.png?w=128&amp;h=18 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image23.png?w=300&amp;h=41 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image23.png?w=768&amp;h=106 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image23.png?w=1024&amp;h=141 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1244px) 100vw, 1244px" /></a></figure></div>


<p></p>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">4.8. Deleting Shadow Copies</h5>



<p>By calling <strong><code>IsWow64Process</code></strong>, Pandora checks if its process is running under a 64-bit system. If it is, then it calls <code><strong>Wow64DisableWow64FsRedirection</strong> </code>to disable file system redirection for its process. Finally, it calls <code><strong>ShellExecuteW</strong> </code>to launch a command for deleting all shadow copies:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image24.png"><img data-attachment-id="6220" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image24/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image24.png" data-orig-size="1267,295" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image24" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image24.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image24.png?w=1267" loading="lazy" width="1267" height="295" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image24.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6220" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image24.png 1267w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image24.png?w=128&amp;h=30 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image24.png?w=300&amp;h=70 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image24.png?w=768&amp;h=179 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image24.png?w=1024&amp;h=238 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1267px) 100vw, 1267px" /></a></figure></div>


<p>The command is:</p>


<div class="wp-block-syntaxhighlighter-code "><pre class="brush: cpp; title: ; notranslate" title="">
cmd.exe "/c vssadmin.exe delete shadows /all /quiet"
</pre></div>


<p></p>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">4.9. Manually mount drives</h5>



<p>Pandora provides a built-in list of drive letters:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image25.png"><img data-attachment-id="6223" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image25/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image25.png" data-orig-size="1307,187" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image25" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image25.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image25.png?w=1307" loading="lazy" width="1307" height="187" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image25.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6223" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image25.png 1307w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image25.png?w=128&amp;h=18 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image25.png?w=300&amp;h=43 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image25.png?w=768&amp;h=110 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image25.png?w=1024&amp;h=147 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1307px) 100vw, 1307px" /></a></figure></div>

<p>Then it uses the function <strong><code>GetDriveTypeW </code></strong>to find drives with type <strong><code>DRIVE_NO_ROOT_DIR</code></strong>.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image26.png"><img data-attachment-id="6225" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image26/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image26.png" data-orig-size="983,386" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image26" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image26.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image26.png?w=983" loading="lazy" width="983" height="386" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image26.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6225" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image26.png 983w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image26.png?w=128&amp;h=50 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image26.png?w=300&amp;h=118 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image26.png?w=768&amp;h=302 768w" sizes="(max-width: 983px) 100vw, 983px" /></a></figure>



<p>Next Pandora calls the <strong><code>FindFirstVolumeW</code></strong>, <strong><code>GetVolumePathNamesForVolumeNameW</code></strong>, <strong><code>SetVolumeMountPointW</code></strong>, <strong><code>FindNextVolumeW </code></strong>functions to mount the drives.</p>



<p></p>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">4.10. Drop ransom note</h5>



<p>Pandora decrypts the ransom note, then writes it to a file named R<strong><code>estore_My_Files.txt</code></strong>:</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image27.png"><img data-attachment-id="6228" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image27/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image27.png" data-orig-size="1690,652" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image27" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image27.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image27.png?w=1690" loading="lazy" width="1690" height="652" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image27.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6228" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image27.png 1690w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image27.png?w=128&amp;h=49 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image27.png?w=300&amp;h=116 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image27.png?w=768&amp;h=296 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image27.png?w=1024&amp;h=395 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1690px) 100vw, 1690px" /></a></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_ransom_notes_string.png"><img data-attachment-id="6229" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/decrypt_ransom_notes_string/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_ransom_notes_string.png" data-orig-size="1830,788" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="decrypt_ransom_notes_string" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_ransom_notes_string.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_ransom_notes_string.png?w=1830" loading="lazy" width="1830" height="788" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_ransom_notes_string.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6229" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_ransom_notes_string.png 1830w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_ransom_notes_string.png?w=128&amp;h=55 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_ransom_notes_string.png?w=300&amp;h=129 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_ransom_notes_string.png?w=768&amp;h=331 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/decrypt_ransom_notes_string.png?w=1024&amp;h=441 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1830px) 100vw, 1830px" /></a></figure></div>


<p>The full content of Ransom note is as follows:</p>


<div class="wp-block-syntaxhighlighter-code "><pre class="brush: cpp; title: ; notranslate" title="">
### What happened?
#### !!!Your files are encrypted!!!
*All your files are protected by strong encryption with RSA-2048.*
*There is no public decryption software.*
*We have successfully stolen your confidential document data, finances, emails, employee information, customers, research and development products...*
#### What is the price?
*The price depends on how fast you can write to us.*
*After payment, we will send you the decryption tool which will decrypt all your files.*
#### What should I do?

*There is only one way to get your files back --&gt;&gt;Contact us, pay and get decryption software.*
*If you decline payment, we will share your data files with the world.*
*You can browse your data breach here: http://vbfqeh5nugm6r2u2qvghsdxm3fotf5wbxb5ltv6vw77vus5frdpuaiid.onion*
(you should download and install TOR browser first hxxps://torproject.org)
#### !!!Decryption Guaranteed!!!
*Free decryption As a guarantee, you can send us up to 3 free decrypted files before payment.*
#### !!!Contact us!!!
email:
contact@pandoraxyz.xyz
#### !!!Warning!!!
*Do not attempt to decrypt your data using third-party software, this may result in permanent data loss.*
*Decrypting your files with the help of a third party may result in a price increase (they charge us a fee), or you may fall victim to a scam.*
*Don&#039;t try to delete programs or run antivirus tools. It won&#039;t work.*
*Attempting to self-decrypt the file will result in the loss of your data.*
</pre></div>


<p></p>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">4.11. List of file extension and directories to avoid</h5>



<p class="has-text-align-justify">Before performing encryption, Pandora will check if the filename is not in the list of files and directories to avoid.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><a href="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image28.png"><img data-attachment-id="6232" data-permalink="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/image28/" data-orig-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image28.png" data-orig-size="1321,194" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="image28" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image28.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image28.png?w=1321" loading="lazy" width="1321" height="194" src="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image28.png" alt="" class="wp-image-6232" srcset="https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image28.png 1321w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image28.png?w=128&amp;h=19 128w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image28.png?w=300&amp;h=44 300w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image28.png?w=768&amp;h=113 768w, https://kienmanowar.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/image28.png?w=1024&amp;h=150 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1321px) 100vw, 1321px" /></a></figure>

					const postEndpoint = `https://wordpress.com/post`;

						) {

						}
					};

					if ( /Firefox/.test( navigator.userAgent ) ) {

					} else {

			fetchExternalScript('verbum');

			if (!loaders[handle]) {
				console.error('WP_Enqueue_Dynamic_Script: unregistered script `' + handle + '`.');
			}
			return loaders[handle]();
		}
	};

			return Promise.resolve();
		}

		fetches[handle] = fetches[handle] || fetch(urls[handle], { mode: 'no-cors' });
		return fetches[handle];
	}

	function runExtraScript(handle, type, index) {
		const id = 'wp-enqueue-dynamic-script:' + handle + ':' + type + ':' + (index + 1);
		const template = document.getElementById(id);
		if (!template) {
			return Promise.reject();
		}

		const script = document.createElement( 'script' );
		script.innerHTML = template.innerHTML;
		document.body.appendChild( script );
		return Promise.resolve();
	}

	function loadExternalScript(handle) {
		if (!urls[handle]) {
			return Promise.resolve();
		}

		return fetches[handle].then(() => {
			return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
				const script = document.createElement('script');
				script.onload = () => resolve();
				script.onerror = (e) => reject(e);
				script.src = urls[handle];
				document.body.appendChild(script);
			});
		});
	}

	function loadExtra(handle, pos) {
		const count = (scriptExtras[handle] && scriptExtras[handle][pos]) || 0;
		let promise = Promise.resolve();

		for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
			promise = promise.then(() => runExtraScript(handle, pos, i));
		}

		return promise;
	}

	function loadWPScript(handle) {
		// Core loads scripts in this order. See: https://github.com/WordPress/WordPress/blob/a59eb9d39c4fcba834b70c9e8dfd64feeec10ba6/wp-includes/class-wp-scripts.php#L428.
		return loadExtra(handle, 'translations')
			.then(() => loadExtra(handle, 'before'))
			.then(() => loadExternalScript(handle))
			.then(() => loadExtra(handle, 'after'));
	}
} )();
</script>
</body>
</html>
